      210 +Each folder has one job:                                      
      211  
      149 -## Design Principles                                          
      212 +| Folder | Responsibility | When Used |                       
      213 +|--------|----------------|-----------|                       
      214 +| `ionic/` | Cell model equations | Shared by both paradigms |
      215 +| `tissue_builder/` | Create geometry, matrices, stimulus | In
          +it time only |                                                
      216 +| `simulation/classical/state.py` | Store all runtime data | R
          +untime |                                                      
      217 +| `simulation/classical/solver/` | Advance time (FEM/FDM path)
          + | Runtime |                                                  
      218 +| `simulation/lbm/` | Self-contained LBM alternative | Runtime
          + |                                                            
      219 +| `utils/` | Device management | Throughout |                 
      220  
      151 -### 1. Physics vs Numerics vs Hardware                        
      221 +---                                                           
      222  
      153 -```                                                           
      154 -                        Biology   Numerics   Hardware   Data  
      155 -                        в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ   в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ   в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ   в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ  
      156 -ionic/models/             вң“                                   
      157 -solver/ionic/                        вң“                        
      158 -solver/diffusion/                    вң“                        
      159 -solver/splitting/                    вң“                        
          -(ordering)                                                    
      160 -solver/__init__.py                   вң“                        
          -(dispatch + stimulus)                                         
      161 -simulation/monodomain.py                                      
          -(orchestration)                                               
      162 -simulation/state.py                                     вң“     
      163 -utils/backend.py                                вң“             
      164 -utils/platform.py                               вң“             
          -(strategy bridge)                                             
      165 -```                                                           
      223 +## Two Simulation Paradigms                                   
      224  
      167 -### 2. Ionic Models Are Data Providers Only                   
      225 +### Classical (FEM/FDM/FVM)                                   
      226  
      169 -Models provide **computation functions**. They do not control 
          -stepping strategy.                                            
      227 +Traditional PDE-based approach:                               
      228 +1. Spatial discretization creates matrices (M, K)             
      229 +2. Time stepping solves linear systems                        
      230 +3. Requires linear solvers (PCG, Chebyshev, etc.)             
      231  
      232  ```
      172 -ionic/base.py defines:              solver/ decides:          
      173 -в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ               в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җ        
      174 -compute_Iion()                      When to call Iion         
      175 -compute_gate_steady_states()        Rush-Larsen or Euler for g
          -ates                                                          
      176 -compute_gate_time_constants()       dt size and substep count 
      177 -compute_concentration_rates()       Splitting order           
      178 -get_initial_state()                 Godunov or Strang         
      179 -```                                                           
      233 +tissue_builder/     вҶ’     state.py     вҶ’     solver/          
      234 +   (build)               (store)            (compute)         
      235  
      181 -### 3. One File Per Method                                    
      182 -                                                              
      183 -Each solver/strategy is self-contained in a single file. Addin
          -g a new one means adding one file вҖ” no existing files change. 
      184 -                                                              
      236 +   [init]                [init]             [runtime]         
      237  ```
      186 -Adding a new ionic solver:        Adding a new splitting strat
          -egy:                                                          
      187 -1. Create ionic/hybrid_imex.py    1. Create splitting/lie_trot
          -ter.py                                                        
      188 -2. Implement IonicSolver ABC      2. Implement SplittingStrate
          -gy ABC                                                        
      189 -3. Done.                          3. Done.                    
      190 -```                                                           
      238  
      192 -### 4. Solver Owns Stimulus                                   
      239 +### Lattice-Boltzmann (LBM)                                   
      240  
      194 -The solver is the "complete timestep unit." Stimulus is part o
          -f what happens in one dt, so the solver owns it. Strategy file
          -s remain unaware of stimulus вҖ” they receive Istim as a tensor.
      241 +Alternative paradigm:                                         
      242 +1. Works on Cartesian grids                                   
      243 +2. Collision + streaming steps (no linear solve)              
      244 +3. Self-contained, highly parallel                            
      245 +4. 10-45Г— faster than FEM (see LBM-EP paper)                  
      246  
      247  ```
      197 -monodomain.py: "Do one timestep."                             
      198 -    в”Ӯ                                                         
      199 -    в””в”Җв”Җв–ә solver: "I'll handle stimulus + ionic + diffusion."  
      200 -            в”Ӯ                                                 
      201 -            в”ңв”Җв”Җ stimulus.get_current(t) вҶ’ Istim               
      202 -            в”Ӯ                                                 
      203 -            в””в”Җв”Җ strategy.execute(..., Istim)                  
      204 -                    в”Ӯ                                         
      205 -                    в”ңв”Җв”Җ ionic.solve(..., Istim)     вҶҗ receives
          - Istim

      757 -## Side-by-Side Comparison                                    
      508 +## User API                                                   
      509  
      759 -| Aspect | Current | Proposed | Improvement |                 
      760 -|--------|---------|----------|-------------|                 
      761 -| **Mesh location** | `fem/mesh.py` | `tissue/mesh.py` | Group
          -s spatial concerns together |                                 
      762 -| **Discretization** | FEM only | FEM/FDM/FVM pluggable | Exte
          -nsible to new methods |                                       
      763 -| **LUT location** | `ionic/lut.py` | `ionic/models/lut.py` | 
          -Co-located with models it serves |                            
      764 -| **Simulation** | Inside `tissue/` | Top-level `simulation/` 
          -| Clear entry point |                                         
      765 -| **step() location** | Inside each ionic model | `solver/ioni
          -c/` | Physics separated from numerics |                       
      766 -| **Linear solver** | Top-level `solver/` | `solver/diffusion/
          -pcg.py` | Grouped with what it serves |                       
      767 -| **Splitting strategy** | Hardcoded Godunov | `solver/splitti
          -ng/{method}.py` | Swappable, one file each |                  
      768 -| **Stimulus ownership** | `tissue/stimulus.py` | Solver owns,
          - `stimulus.py` defines | Part of timestep unit |              
      769 -| **Adding a solver** | Edit existing files | Add one new file
          - | Open-closed principle |                                    
      770 -| **Ionic model role** | Physics + stepping | Physics only (da
          -ta provider) | Single responsibility |                        
      510 +### Classical Approach                                        
      511

      615  
      616 +## Lattice-Boltzmann Method                                   
      617 +                                                              
      618 +LBM is a fundamentally different paradigm вҖ” it doesn't fit int
          +o the "spatial discretization + time integration + linear solv
          +er" hierarchy.                                                
      619 +                                                              
      620 +### How LBM Works                                             
      621 +                                                              
      622 +Instead of discretizing the PDE and solving linear systems, LB
          +M works with distribution functions:                          
      623 +                                                              
      624 +```                                                           
      625 +1. COLLISION (local relaxation):                              
      626 +   f*_i = f_i - A_ij(f_j - Пү_jВ·v) + ОҙtВ·Пү_iВ·(J_in + J_out + J_s
          +tim)                                                          
      627 +                                                              
      628 +2. STREAMING (shift to neighbors):                            
      629 +   f_i(x + e_i, t + Оҙt) = f*_i(x, t)                          
      630 +                                                              
      631 +3. RECOVER POTENTIAL:                                         
      632 +   v = ОЈ f_i                                                  
      633 +```                                                           
      634 +                                                              
      635 +### LBM Characteristics                                       
      636 +                                                              
      637 +| Property | LBM | Classical (FEM) |                          
      638 +|----------|-----|-----------------|                          
      639 +| Linear solver needed | **No** | Yes (implicit) |            
      640 +| Mesh required | Cartesian grid only | Various |             
      641 +| Parallelism | Embarrassingly parallel | Depends on solver | 
      642 +| Time stepping | Built-in | Separate choice |                
      643 +| Speed | **10-45Г— faster** | Baseline |                      
      644 +                                                              
      645 +### LBM is Independent                                        
      646 +                                                              
      647 +LBM doesn't use `tissue_builder/discretization/` or `solver/`.
          + It has its own complete implementation in `simulation/lbm/`. 
      648 +                                                              
      649 +---                                                           
      650 +                                                              
      651 +## File Responsibility Matrix                                 
      652 +                                                              
      653 +```                                                           
      654 +FILE                                              OWNS        
          +        KNOWS / DECIDES

      696  
      697  The proposed architecture improves the codebase by:
      698  
      699 +- **Separating builders from storage** вҖ” `tissue_builder/` cre
          +ates data, `state.py` stores it                               
      700 +- **Two simulation paradigms** вҖ” `classical/` (FEM/FDM) and `l
          +bm/` (Lattice-Boltzmann)                                      
      701  - **Separating physics from numerics** вҖ” ionic models provide 
           computation functions, solvers decide how to use them
      943 -- **One file per method** вҖ” adding a new solver or splitting s
          -trategy is adding one file, no existing files change          
      944 -- **Solver as complete timestep unit** вҖ” `solver/` owns stimul
          -us, splitting, ionic, and diffusion                           
      945 -- **Three parallel solver concerns** вҖ” `splitting/`, `ionic/`,
          - `diffusion/` each handle one concept                         
      946 -- **Strategy files stay pure** вҖ” splitting strategies receive 
          -Istim, don't know about stimulus                              
      947 -- **Thin monodomain.py** вҖ” only loop, save, progress, and user
          - API                                                          
      948 -- **Grouping mesh with tissue** вҖ” spatial concerns belong toge
          -ther                                                          
      949 -- **Enabling multiple discretization methods** вҖ” FEM, FDM, FVM
          - pluggable                                                    
      950 -- **Co-locating LUT with models** вҖ” lookup tables sit next to 
          -the models they accelerate                                    
      951 -- **Platform-aware GPU optimization** вҖ” `utils/platform.py` pr
          -ovides frozen `PlatformProfile` per hardware (CUDA, MPS, CPU),
          - auto-detected at init and consumed by all solver components  
      952 -- **Clean responsibility boundaries** вҖ” each file has one reas
          -on to change                                                  
      702 +- **Explicit/implicit split** вҖ” `diffusion_time_stepping/expli
          +cit/` vs `implicit/` with `linear_solver/`                    
      703 +- **One file per method** вҖ” adding a new solver or splitting s
          +trategy is adding one file                                    
      704 +- **GPU-friendly options** вҖ” Chebyshev solver, fixed-iteration
          + PCG, output buffering                                        
      705 +- **Clear responsibility boundaries** вҖ” each file has one reas
          +on to change                                                  
      706 +- **Extensible to new methods** вҖ” FDM, FVM, RK2/4, multigrid, 
          +FFT all have clear homes
